For a 40-year-old Obasan who has worked for 20 years, it would definitely not be appropriate for you to apply the standards of a 20-year-old girl.

The Jinshi Hotel belongs to that kind of 60-year-old woman who has worked for 30 years, has a wrinkled face, is skinny, and has sex, and still wants to rely on her reputation in her youth to attract customers.

Personally, I usually stay in Nantong. Most of the time it is mainly intercontinental. However, Intercontinental also has an unavoidable shortcoming: it is too remote.

I checked in on the 14th, and it snowed heavily in North China that day. The high-speed train was supposed to leave at four o'clock in the afternoon, but I didn't get on the train until nine o'clock. I didn't arrive in Nantong until 1:30 in the morning. It's not realistic for me to ask for a car to take me to the Intercontinental from Nantong Station at 1:30 in the morning. Just thinking about it, I stayed in Jinshi several times a few years ago and it should be okay. Anyway, itâ€™s just for one night. Not too trashy.

However, this time the nausea came. I wanted to take a short rest and rush home. So I am not happy to spend how much money to book a room that is too good. Jinshi initially called to tell us that the room had been upgraded. I want to thank you. I went to the room at two o'clock in the morning and fell asleep. I didn't even think about it. Even though it had a five-star brand name and was one of the best in Nantong City in the past, the bedding was still bad.

This lasted until the next day, when the guest room came to be cleaned, an aunt told me. I just know. Regarding this bedding issue, Manager Cui at the front desk and Jason from the guest room did make a special trip to apologize. This is worthy of recognition.

What about the bedding issue. Just pass it by for now. The next day, because I had something to do at home, I couldn't renew my subscription for another day. Because I arrived at the store early in the morning, I didn't want to take a shower. I got up during the day and thought I would definitely take a shower in the future. Taking a shower and taking a shower will clear up more problems.

First, this bathroom door. It is difficult to push away easily. After I took a shower, I stood inside and couldn't push the door open with normal strength. When the force is strong, the door will make a loud banging sound. I'm afraid it's such an old hotel and it's a big winter. What if the glass door explodes? It's easy to talk about these trivial things in hotels, but once you get hurt in your life by them, haha.

I myself am anxious to go home. Anyway, I didn't do any harm. I'm not happy to argue with Jin Shi either. As for the metal stone, it was just right anyway. I originally asked the engineering depar**ent to come and repair it, but after waiting for half an hour, I didn't see the ghost of the engineering depar**ent.

Secondly, the water pressure of the bathroom nozzle is too high, and the water spray on the body is like a sharp knife piercing the body.

There is still 2023, almost today in 2024. Basically, some high-end hotels use Dyson hair dryers. Even if you canâ€™t afford Dyson, I can still give you an imitation version. The stone is ready. The hair dryer in my room looks older than my dog.

With these services, the shortcomings of the facilities can be basically ignored.
Environment: The high-rise river view room is given, and the night view of the Yangtze River is good. The hotel location is also good.
